1944         op ^= \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_ae26952ba9cd5bea1e4bdcf9eb42ce545}{SLJIT\_F32\_OP};
1945 
1946     dst\_r = \hyperlink{sljitLir_8c_a6bbf8427bd58f7ae7c518580ceaaa9b4}{FAST\_IS\_REG}(dst) ? dst : \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_ae348729da082f19b0da18064637d6ac8}{TMP\_FREG1};
1947 
1948     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__PROTO_ga3250c7d76063d957a24f2ecbb3d93c2c}{src} & \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_ac3bd7a51e6dcd2084265caa93a342cd7}{SLJIT\_MEM}) \{
1949         \hyperlink{sljitLir_8c_ac3f0b0a9b2ff97cbc870e69a7dfa590b}{FAIL\_IF}(emit\_op\_mem2(compiler, \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_a1cfcc5a176634667b945f662b1389800}{FLOAT\_DATA}(op) | 
      \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_ab39cfd238f2c6799c71d5a62703a93fa}{LOAD\_DATA}, dst\_r, \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__PROTO_ga3250c7d76063d957a24f2ecbb3d93c2c}{src}, srcw, dst, dstw));
1950         \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__PROTO_ga3250c7d76063d957a24f2ecbb3d93c2c}{src} = dst\_r;
1951     \}
1952 
1953     \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (\hyperlink{sljitLir_8c_ac8bcbde5788ae997737284022e42ad92}{GET\_OPCODE}(op)) \{
1954     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_ada5b30fe6ed416b7903102c234aa3a5e}{SLJIT\_CONV\_F64\_FROM\_F32}:
1955         op ^= \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_ae26952ba9cd5bea1e4bdcf9eb42ce545}{SLJIT\_F32\_OP};
1956         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (op & \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_ae26952ba9cd5bea1e4bdcf9eb42ce545}{SLJIT\_F32\_OP}) \{
1957             \hyperlink{sljitLir_8c_ac3f0b0a9b2ff97cbc870e69a7dfa590b}{FAIL\_IF}(push\_inst(compiler, \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_a64afc00fcaeebc470aa2c5132dadb542}{FRSP} | \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_a6321199f956a67161993814f11e406ed}{FD}(dst\_r) | \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_abc41204434d982e3126e23e6657c7197}{FB}(\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__PROTO_ga3250c7d76063d957a24f2ecbb3d93c2c}{src})));
1958             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
1959         \}
1960         \textcolor{comment}{/* Fall through. */}
1961     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_a976dc0e5e8a377002d8f818e2b2c0f81}{SLJIT\_MOV\_F64}:
1962         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__PROTO_ga3250c7d76063d957a24f2ecbb3d93c2c}{src} != dst\_r) \{
1963             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dst\_r != \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_ae348729da082f19b0da18064637d6ac8}{TMP\_FREG1})
1964                 \hyperlink{sljitLir_8c_ac3f0b0a9b2ff97cbc870e69a7dfa590b}{FAIL\_IF}(push\_inst(compiler, \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_afcf966ea3b3c937d162a532a8f273cae}{FMR} | \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_a6321199f956a67161993814f11e406ed}{FD}(dst\_r) | \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_abc41204434d982e3126e23e6657c7197}{FB}(
      \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__PROTO_ga3250c7d76063d957a24f2ecbb3d93c2c}{src})));
1965             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
1966                 dst\_r = \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__PROTO_ga3250c7d76063d957a24f2ecbb3d93c2c}{src};
1967         \}
1968         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
1969     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_af2df647f9c6cc3833c506c54ed0d67e1}{SLJIT\_NEG\_F64}:
1970         \hyperlink{sljitLir_8c_ac3f0b0a9b2ff97cbc870e69a7dfa590b}{FAIL\_IF}(push\_inst(compiler, \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_a8df769cda2c11d875fa68eaad65ba75f}{FNEG} | \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_a6321199f956a67161993814f11e406ed}{FD}(dst\_r) | \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_abc41204434d982e3126e23e6657c7197}{FB}(\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__PROTO_ga3250c7d76063d957a24f2ecbb3d93c2c}{src})));
1971         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
1972     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_a51ac468bbd03dd41a294b41a15a6624a}{SLJIT\_ABS\_F64}:
1973         \hyperlink{sljitLir_8c_ac3f0b0a9b2ff97cbc870e69a7dfa590b}{FAIL\_IF}(push\_inst(compiler, \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_af0175ba905b01f1a4ba753b6961473c5}{FABS} | \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_a6321199f956a67161993814f11e406ed}{FD}(dst\_r) | \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_abc41204434d982e3126e23e6657c7197}{FB}(\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__PROTO_ga3250c7d76063d957a24f2ecbb3d93c2c}{src})));
1974         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
1975     \}
1976 
1977     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dst & SLJIT\_MEM)
1978         \hyperlink{sljitLir_8c_ac3f0b0a9b2ff97cbc870e69a7dfa590b}{FAIL\_IF}(emit\_op\_mem2(compiler, \hyperlink{sljitNativePPC__common_8c_a1cfcc5a176634667b945f662b1389800}{FLOAT\_DATA}(op), dst\_r, dst, dstw, 0, 0));
1979     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{sljitLir_8h_a70ae3a25ae80f24318b4fd0f82995f9b}{SLJIT\_SUCCESS};
1980 \}
